FROM (
    SELECT "p"."Id", "p"."CreationDate", "p"."Title", "p"."UserId", "u"."Id" AS "Id0", "u"."DateOfBirth", "u"."Email", "u"."Password", "u"."Username"
    FROM "Playlists" AS "p"
    INNER JOIN "Users" AS "u" ON "p"."UserId" = "u"."Id"
    WHERE "p"."Id" = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS "s0"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT "p0"."PlaylistId", "p0"."SongId", "s"."Id", "s"."AlbumId", "s"."Duration", "s"."Genre", "s"."ReleaseDate", "s"."Title", "a"."Id" AS "Id0", "a"."ArtistId", "a"."Genre" AS "Genre0", "a"."ReleaseYear", "a"."Title" AS "Title0", "a0"."Id" AS "Id1", "a0"."Genre" AS "Genre1", "a0"."Name"
    FROM "PlaylistSongs" AS "p0"
    INNER JOIN "Songs" AS "s" ON "p0"."SongId" = "s"."Id"
    INNER JOIN "Albums" AS "a" ON "s"."AlbumId" = "a"."Id"
    INNER JOIN "Artists" AS "a0" ON "a"."ArtistId" = "a0"."Id"
) AS "s1" ON "s0"."Id" = "s1"."PlaylistId"
ORDER BY "s0"."Id", "s0"."Id0", "s1"."PlaylistId", "s1"."SongId", "s1"."Id", "s1"."Id0"
